		factor = 100
	}

		country_event = solar.137
		if = {
			limit = {

			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

			}
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
			    has_idea = limited_conscription 
			}
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
			    has_idea = extensive_conscription 
			}

		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 55 }

shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_mandatory_sacrifice
	x = 1
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = EQS_force_sides_together
	
	bypass = { has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation }
	
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = {
		focus = EQS_counsel_councilors
		focus = EQS_lonely_top
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = EQS_force_sides_together
		focus = EQS_tighten_loins
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_mandatory_sacrifice"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = civilian_economy }
			add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation }
			add_ideas = partial_economic_mobilisation
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation }
			add_ideas = war_economy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = war_economy }
			add_ideas = tot_economic_mobilisation
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 60 }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_reborn_heartland
	x = 0
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = EQS_holy_flame
	
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_new_religion }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_holy_flame }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_monuments_to_victory }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_conscript_the_masses }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_expatriate_issue }
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_reborn_heartland"
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = WHY
					is_core_of = BLS
					is_core_of = NER
					is_core_of = CER
					is_core_of = CLD
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { has_country_flag = EQS_harsh_punishment }
				}
				add_resistance_target = -10
			}
			ELSE_IF = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = EQS_flexible_punishment } }
				add_resistance_target = -3.5
				add_compliance = 7.5
			}
			ELSE = {
				add_resistance = -5
				add_compliance = 12.5
			}
		}
		set_province_name = { id = 782 name = renamed_new_canterlot }
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_variable = { equestria_conquest = 1 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 60 }
}

					}

		add_stability = 0.03
	}

	id = EQS_the_gravest_of_errors_the_greatest_of_comebacks
	x = -6
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_march_toward_communism
	
	bypass = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = EQS_BAL_dead_tt
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = balsplosion
						country_exists = BAL
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = balsplosion
					NOT = {
						country_exists = MTS
						country_exists = EEE
						country_exists = NID
						country_exists = NEI
						country_exists = CLI
						country_exists = SPF
						country_exists = STB
						country_exists = NRP
						country_exists = BAL
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cost = 3
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_march_toward_communism }
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_the_gravest_of_errors_the_greatest_of_comebacks"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = global.southeast_countries
					value = THIS
				}
			}
		
			EQS = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 60 }
}

		}

		}

				create_wargoal = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_from_guns_to_plowshares
	x = -1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_mercy_is_for_the_forgiven
	
	available = {
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = CHN
			}
			has_war = no
		}
	}
	
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_mercy_is_for_the_forgiven }
	
	select_effect = {
		IF = {
			limit = { check_variable = { equestria_conquest = 5 } }
			set_variable = { equestria_conquest = 11 } #Changelings conquered and CRY conquered before STG
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			limit = { check_variable = { equestria_conquest = 4 } } #Stalliongrad conquered first
			set_variable = { equestria_conquest = 12 }
		}
		ELSE = {
			set_variable = { equestria_conquest = 10 }
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_from_guns_to_plowshares"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = EQS_swords_into_plowshares
			days = 90
		}
		###Add timed idea for 15% increased factory and dockyard output for 90 days
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
}

	id = EQS_a_lesson_in_humility
	x = -4
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_solaris_quorundam
	
	bypass = {
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = CLD
				country_exists = NER
			}
		}
	}
	
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_solaris_quorundam }
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_a_lesson_in_humility"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NER
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = NER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CLD
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = CLD
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 25 }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_no_mercy_for_the_wicked
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_remove_the_military_from_power
	
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_remove_the_military_from_power }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_faith_triumphs_over_atheism }
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_no_mercy_for_the_wicked"
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					is_core_of = BLS
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_manpower = -37500
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					is_core_of = WHY
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_manpower = -25000
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 28 }
}

###Stalliongrad War###
shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_opportunistic_rats
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_brothers_and_sisters_in_the_empress
	
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_brothers_and_sisters_in_the_empress }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_further_streamlining }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_reminding_the_militarium_of_its_place }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = EQS_to_the_land_of_darkness }
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_opportunistic_rats"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = STG
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 3
				name = EQS_stalliongrad_war
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = EQS_war_with_southeast_two_weeks
		set_country_flag = EQS_southeast_war_prep
		###Initiate timer for attacking in fourteen days
		#IF = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_global_flag = SOL_stalliongrad_war
		#	}
		#	country_event = solar.337
		#	###Country event for Aurora learning of Stalliongrad's imminent war and making the Empire go into an emergency
		#}
		#ELSE = {
		#	country_event = solar.338
		#}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
	}
}

###Southeast war###
shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_to_the_land_of_darkness
	x = 3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_brothers_and_sisters_in_the_empress
	
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = balsplosion
					country_exists = BAL
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = balsplosion
				NOT = {
					country_exists = MTS
					country_exists = EEE
					country_exists = NID
					country_exists = NEI
					country_exists = CLI
					country_exists = SPF
					country_exists = STB
					country_exists = NRP
					country_exists = BAL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_brothers_and_sisters_in_the_empress }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_further_streamlining }
	prerequisite = { focus = EQS_reminding_the_militarium_of_its_place }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = EQS_opportunistic_rats }
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_to_the_land_of_darkness"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = global.southeast_countries
					value = THIS
				}
			}
		
			EQS = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			###Initiate timer for war with STG in two weeks
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = EQS_stg_war_two_weeks
		set_country_flag = EQS_stg_prep
		hidden_effect = {
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 3
				name = EQS_southeast_war
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
		modifier = { has_global_flag = balsplosion factor = 2.5 }
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = EQS_rain_hellfire_upon_them
	x = 2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = EQS_to_the_land_of_darkness
	
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = balsplosion
					country_exists = BAL
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = balsplosion
				NOT = {
					country_exists = MTS
					country_exists = EEE
					country_exists = NID
					country_exists = NEI
					country_exists = CLI
					country_exists = SPF
					country_exists = STB
					country_exists = NRP
					country_exists = BAL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = EQS_opportunistic_rats 
		focus = EQS_to_the_land_of_darkness
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus EQS_rain_hellfire_upon_them"
		29 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = air_base
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Meurom Mangler"
				type = small_plane_cas_airframe_1
				modules = {
					fixed_main_weapon_slot = bomb_locks
					fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_1 = bomb_locks
					engine_type_slot = engine_2_1x
					special_type_slot_1 = drop_tanks
					special_type_slot_2 = empty
				}
				icon = "GFX_ENG_CAS1_medium"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_cas_airframe
				amount = 500
				producer = EQS
				variant = "Meurom Mangler"
			}
		}
		ELSE = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_cas_airframe

				producer = EQS
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 28 }
}
